p = int(input())
keta = len(n)
Dp = [[[0 for _ in range(2)] for _ in range(keta+1)] for _ in range(keta+1)]

    j = 0
    while j <= i:
        k = 0
        while k < 10:

            if k == 0:

                    Dp[i+1][j][0] += Dp[i][j][0]
                    Dp[i+1][j][0] += Dp[i][j][1]

                    Dp[i+1][j][0] += Dp[i][j][0]

                if k < digit:
                    Dp[i+1][j+1][0] += Dp[i][j][0]
                    Dp[i+1][j+1][0] += Dp[i][j][1]
                elif k == digit:
                    Dp[i+1][j+1][1] += Dp[i][j][1]
                    Dp[i+1][j+1][0] += Dp[i][j][0]
                else:
                    Dp[i+1][j+1][0] += Dp[i][j][0]
            k += 1
        j += 1
    i += 1

    print(0)
